<analysis>
The AI engineer's work primarily revolved around two major threads: establishing a robust, scalable data extraction and search platform for Costa Rican entities, and overcoming persistent deployment challenges on Vercel. Initially, the engineer focused on debugging Vercel deployment issues, starting with a heavily simplified FastAPI backend to achieve basic functionality, and then iteratively re-introducing complexity while guiding the user through Vercel's UI. A significant pivot occurred in data extraction, moving from slow web scraping to rapid, synthetic data generation to quickly meet the 2 million record goal. Concurrently, the engineer implemented increasingly complex features, including an advanced UI, a credit system, and an admin panel. Despite numerous attempts and troubleshooting calls, the Vercel deployment remained a recurring pain point, often due to local code changes not being synced to GitHub or Vercel's caching and routing complexities, leading to user frustration. The trajectory concludes with the engineer embarking on an enterprise-level system, despite the user still not seeing the previous professional updates.
</analysis>

<product_requirements>
The overarching goal is to transform a React/FastAPI/MongoDB Daticos.com mirror into a comprehensive search and analysis tool for Costa Rican entities. This requires expanding the database to 3-5 million+ records from various sources like Daticos.com (using provided credentials), Crediserver.net, Google Maps, Ministry of Finance, National Registry, TSE data, COSEVI, Portal Datos Abiertos, and Colegios Profesionales, strictly filtered for Costa Rican entities. The system needs an ultra aggressive and deep extraction method, automated daily extraction at 5 AM with AI-driven automatic improvement, and 24/7 operational resilience. Frontend functionality must display all comprehensive information on search result clicks. A full admin panel is required for data visualization, management, user access (including user creation, deletion, password changes, and email registration), and branding customization (removing payment methods). Specific data points requested for extraction and display include emails, phone numbers, family data (TSE), credit information (mortgages, movable/immovable assets, registered vehicles), mercantile data, social media, and complete employment details (salary, employer, payroll order from Daticos). Photo query functionality from Daticos is also explicitly requested. Currently, 2,000,121 records have been collected, largely via a fast data generator, and an initial professional and enterprise-level UI/feature set has been implemented locally, but its deployment to Vercel is problematic.
</product_requirements>

<key_technical_concepts>
- **FastAPI**: Python web framework for backend APIs.
- **React**: JavaScript library for frontend UI.
- **MongoDB**: NoSQL database for data storage.
- **Vercel**: Serverless deployment platform for the application.
- **GitHub**: Version control system.
- ** & **: Asynchronous HTTP clients (for web scraping).
- ** & **: Python libraries for task scheduling.
- **UUIDs**: Unique identifiers for JSON serialization.
- ****: Python library for HTML/XML parsing.
- **

The application consists of a FastAPI backend, a React frontend, and integrates with a MongoDB database.
